### ğŸ”¹ How to Play It Differently  
- **4/4 feel (march / hip-hop):** Count **1-2-3-4** steady.  
  - Guitar: down strums on each beat (chunky, driving).  
  - Drums: kick on 1 & 3, snare on 2 & 4.  
  - Clap: clap on 2 & 4 (â€œthe backbeatâ€).  
  â†’ Feels straight, solid, like walking.  

- **3/4 feel (waltz / sway):** Count **1-2-3**.  
  - Guitar: down-up-down (sway, lighter touch).  
  - Drums: kick on 1, snare or hi-hat on 2 & 3.  
  - Clap: clap only on the â€œ1â€ and sway the body.  
  â†’ Feels circular, dance-like, like swaying in prayer.  

---

### ğŸ”¹ How to Practice Switching  
1. **Clap 4/4 first:** 1-2-3-4, steady.  
2. **Clap 3/4 after:** 1-2-3, 1-2-3, sway.  
3. **Sing the lyrics while clapping.** Youâ€™ll feel the natural shift where the Bridge slows into the waltz.  
4. On guitar, just strum softer in 3/4 â€” itâ€™ll feel like dancing instead of stomping.  

---
